position.coords.longitude;\n\n    var min_distance;\n    var selected = null;\n    jQuery(\"#home-towns li a\").each( function(i, el) {\n      var calculated_distance = distance( jQuery(el).data(\"lat\"), jQuery(el).data(\"lng\"), lat, lng);\n      if( min_distance ) {\n        if (calculated_distance < min_distance) {\n          selected = i;\n          min_distance = calculated_distance;\n        }\n      } else {\n        selected = i;\n        min_distance = calculated_distance;\n      }\n    });\n\n    if( selected ) {\n      jQuery(\"#home-towns li a:eq(\" + selected + \")\").click();\n    }\n  }\n\n  (function($) {\n    if (navigator.geolocation) {\n      navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(selectTown);\n    }\n\n    $(\"#home-towns li a\").on(\"click\", function(event) {\n      $(\"#selected_city\").text($(this).text());\n      $('#destinations_list').append( '<div class=\"loading\"><div class=\"background\"></div><div class=\"spinner-loader\"></div></div>')\n      $.ajax( {\n        method: \"GET\",\n        url: \"/fr/isilines/destination/\" + $(this).data(\"town\")\n      }).done(\n        function(data) {\n          $(\"#destinations_list\").html(data.html);\n        }\n      );\n      event.preventDefault();\n    });\n  })(jQuery)\n</script>\n\n<div class=\"box-multi-infos row main-row clearfix\">\n  <!--
